 83 +                         let shard = engine.shard(shard_id).ok_or_else(|| {
 84 +                             FalconError::internal_bug(
 85 +                                 "E-SCATTER-002",
 86 +                                 format!("Shard {:?} disappeared during execution", shard_id),
 87 +                                 "shard was validated before spawn but missing at execution time",

 95 +                             if attempt > 0 {
 96 +                                 // Interruptible retry delay (condvar instead of bare sleep)
 97 +                                 {
 98 +                                     let pair = std::sync::Mutex::new(false);
 99 +                                     let cvar = std::sync::Condvar::new();
100 +                                     let guard = pair.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
101 +                                     let _ = cvar.wait_timeout(guard, Duration::from_millis(5));
102 +                                 }
103 +                             }
104 + 
105 +                             let start = Instant::now();
106 +                             let result = subplan_ref.execute(&shard.storage, &shard.txn_mgr);
107 +                             let latency_us = start.elapsed().as_micros() as u64;
108 + 
109 +                             // Check timeout
110 +                             if total_start.elapsed() > timeout {
111 +                                 return Err(FalconError::Transient {
112 +                                     reason: format!(
113 +                                         "Scatter/gather timeout after {}ms (shard {:?})",
114 +                                         timeout.as_millis(),
115 +                                         shard_id,
116 +                                     ),
117 +                                     retry_after_ms: 100,
118 +                                 });
119 +                             }
120 + 
121 +                             match result {
122 +                                 Ok((columns, rows)) => {
123 +                                     return Ok(ShardResult {
124 +                                         shard_id,
125 +                                         columns,
126 +                                         rows,
127 +                                         latency_us,
128 +                                     });
129 +                                 }
130 +                                 Err(e) => {
131 +                                     tracing::warn!(
132 +                                         "Shard {:?} attempt {}/{} failed: {}",
133 +                                         shard_id,
134 +                                         attempt + 1,
135 +                                         max_attempts,
136 +                                         e,
137 +                                     );
138 +                                     last_err = Some(e);
139 +                                 }
140 +                             }
141 +                         }
142 + 
143 +                         Err(last_err.unwrap_or_else(|| {
